[3월 10일 소희랑 결혼하면 재밌겠다] [오후 4:11] from datetime import datetime

# Provided timestamps from XML data
start_time_str = "2016-11-04T06:22:48Z"
target_time_str = "2016-11-04T06:23:21Z"

# Convert timestamps to datetime objects
start_time = datetime.strptime(start_time_str, "%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%SZ")
target_time = datetime.strptime(target_time_str, "%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%SZ")

# Calculate the difference in seconds
time_difference = (target_time - start_time).total_seconds()
time_difference


import ffmpeg

# Load the video file
input_video_path = "/mnt/data/output.mp4"
output_frame_path = "/mnt/data/extracted_frame.png"

# Extract the frame at the 33-second mark
ffmpeg.input(input_video_path, ss=33).output(output_frame_path, vframes=1).run(overwrite_output=True)

* 학과 사무실에서는 희망 학생 명단 취합하여 현장실습지원센터로 회신(~8/23)
